lang="EN-US">64</span>岁，辽宁省大连市沙河口区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日晚九点左右，张仁光、王尚杰、韩建海、李静波四人因发真相资料，分别被国保和民权派出所绑架。在张仁光家抄走大量耗材。后全送姚家看守所。大连市沙河口区法院<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日庭审法轮功学员张仁光、王尚杰、韩建海、李静波，并判张仁光<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、勒索罚款两万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张三曼：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">大连市金州区石河镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日晚，谷秀华（女）、刘希永（男）、周兴（男）、李天学（男）、王丽志（女）、张三曼（女）、谭春荣（女）、孙宝英（女）、刘井龙（男），去大连市金普新区炮台镇袁屯村发放新书《共产主义的终极目的》，被炮台镇派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日下午二在大连市金州法院庭审。后谷秀华、周兴、王丽志，被大连市金州法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；张三曼、谭春荣被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，李天学被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，刘希永、孙宝英、刘井龙的情况还不清楚。张三曼刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">张少杰：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1965</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日出生，河南省南乐县人，前河南省南乐县基督教三自爱国运动委员会主席、基督教协会会长，第九届南乐县政协委员，南乐县基督教会牧师，中国在押良心犯。长期以来，因其身为牧师，经常帮助弱势群体维权解难，尤其是当信徒的合法权益受到侵害时，均想法给予及时的帮助与维权，随在当地备受信徒的喜爱，但这种行为却与政府某些人的利益发生冲突，随遭到当局的强烈不满和忌恨；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被南乐县警方在无任何法律手续的前提下强行从教会带走，其两个胞妹在众人的陪同下前去公安局要人，也被警察强行带走，其余人等亦遭警方堵截和殴打，之后才得知张少杰已被当地警方以涉嫌“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，又被追加涉嫌“妨害公务罪”予以批捕，但在起诉书中又显示将“妨害公务罪”变更为“诈骗罪”；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，终被河南省南乐县法院以“诈骗罪”和“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。此前曾先后被羁押在河南省南乐县看守所和濮阳市看守所；目前在河南省新乡市河南第二监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张盛全：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">重庆法轮功学员。重庆市高新区石桥铺人。他原在石桥铺交易城做生意，公平交易，童叟无欺。张盛全曾屡遭中共迫害，他曾被非法劳教两年，在西山坪劳教所遭受过多种酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日重庆<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名法轮功学员张盛全、李嘉惠、李玉华、高洪伟、秦雪美，被抓捕两年多，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月获悉已经被判刑。张盛全、李嘉惠，被枉判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；李玉华<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千元，监外执行；高洪伟<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；秦雪美<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>千元。张盛全刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张淑琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江伊春市法轮功学员，女，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1951</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">，家住伊春市伊春区，在伊春经营一家旅店。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日当地警方对张淑琴经营的旅店进行搜查，并以「利用×教组织破坏法律实施罪」将张淑琴刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，将张淑琴批准逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日伊美区法院对张淑琴开庭审理。张淑琴本人没有到法庭现场，是在看守所以视频方式出庭。律师为张淑琴做了无罪辩护。张淑琴女儿刘春莉也为母亲做了无罪辩护。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张水兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日生，云岭通信器材公司退休职工。张水兰<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年曾经遭受<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年冤狱迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日散发法轮功真相资料遭恶人诬告，被昆明市盘龙区东华派出所警察抓捕、非法抄家，抢走平板计算机一台，及大法书籍、数据等私人物品。后张水兰被昆明市西山区检察院起诉，云南省昆明市西山区法院<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日对昆明市法轮功学员张水兰判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚款</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">10000</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">张素华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">吉林省通化市东昌区法轮功学员，女性，<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁。张素华是<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被通化市警察绑架的，在被非法关押一年半后，于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，在未通知本人律师的情况下被非法开庭的。家属从接到通知到开庭也才不足三小时。当天下午一点半，对张素华非法庭审，整个过程仅用了十分钟，草草收场。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，吉林省通化市东昌区法院对张素华非法判刑七年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张素英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏淮安市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生，张素英<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日左右被淮安<span lang="EN-US">610</span>抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，张素英被清江浦区法院开庭， 一位维权律师出庭做无罪辩护。绑架、非法关押大半年，被淮安市清江浦区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。张素英老人已要求上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">张树德：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">28</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">岁，哈尔滨市双城区新兴乡人，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。自幼练习和笃信法轮功。哈尔滨工业大学毕业后，曾应聘于大连理工设计院，后外派到盘锦市高新技术产业开发区工作，是个诚实、可信、敬业的好青年。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，因居住证到期，张树德到所在地的兴隆台区兴盛派出所办理顺延手续时，当身份证录入相关信息时，警察问他有什么信仰，他称其信仰法轮功，随被拒绝办理居住证，并被威胁要对他调查。三天后，其居室遭搜查，本人被传唤做笔录。<span lang="EN-US"> 6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被双手戴着手铐非法送到盘锦市中心医院检查身体，然后就被强行刑拘于盘锦看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，他被盘锦市公安局兴隆台区分局正式逮捕，并将其案移交到兴隆台区检察院。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，检察院案将其案卷移交到兴隆台区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其案被盘锦市兴隆台区法院开庭受审，至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，张树德被该法院一审枉法重判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，并处罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。其不服上诉。其所在家乡的亲友得知其被冤判后，立刻决定伸出援手征签营救，同乡的父老乡亲们在极短的时间里，亲自填写上自己的名字或按下红手印，呼吁无罪释放张树德回家，目前已有<span lang="EN-US">1744</span>人签名声援。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张顺新：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">新疆喀什地区泽普县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">53</span>岁，在中共对法轮功持续至今近二十年的迫害中，他因修炼法轮功在<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，但他挺过来了。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出狱回家。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日晚十点左右，张顺新被塔西南石油基地公安局（隶属于泽普县公安局）警察冯海洋骗到派出所后，再次被绑架关押抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，新疆喀什地区公安局警察到法轮功学员张顺新家通知亲属，张顺新现被关在农三师图木舒克市盖米里克监狱。亲属这才知道张顺新于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，并在亲属、律师不在场的情况下秘密宣判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张涛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">澳门居民。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，珠海王家婚礼教会牧师魏小妹及丈夫李炳新、同工张涛（澳门居民）被捕。数个月后，珠海市香洲区检察院以“诈骗罪”起诉。控方指魏小妹、李炳新及张涛涉嫌诈骗信徒奉献款，购买房产，构成诈骗罪。据知情人士披露，当局的指控缺乏有力证据，难以成立。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，香洲区民族宗教事务局取缔该教会，并扣留该教会近五十台电脑<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。</b><span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，当局出动数十名公安，拘捕该教会十多名信徒，经过连续审讯及威胁，信徒被迫写下不利于教会领袖的证词。警方最终以诈骗罪刑事拘留该教会牧师魏小妹及丈夫李炳新、同工张涛。据知情人士披露，该案由珠海市政法委督办。当局先以“邪教罪”调查此案，但因查无实据，又改为“诈骗罪”问罪，这明显是一起宗教案件。目前，广东珠海王家婚礼教会牧师魏小妹及丈夫李炳新、同工张涛（澳门居民）三人，被珠海市香洲区检察院以“诈骗罪”起诉至法院，指当事人诈骗奉献款，上述三人面临判刑。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张廷福：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">重庆维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">70</span>多岁老人张廷福在达州下火车，被达州车站派出所拦截扣押后刑事拘留，问其原因，是重庆上清寺派出所将张廷福上传为网上追逃人员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日重庆维权人士张廷福，被重庆市公安局渝中区分局以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑拘，现羁押在渝中区看守所。家属经多方投诉后，才于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日拿到刑事拘留通知书，张廷福也从达州转至重庆渝中区看守所，得知成为逃犯的原因，是派出所以其涉嫌寻衅滋事罪，上传为网上追逃。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">张伟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年生，家住东港市。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日晚，丹东市委、政法委、“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”与丹东市公安局秘密策划，经过长期电话监控以及各种监控手段、跟踪监视，对丹东市公安系统统一部署，丹东国保支队警察倾巢出动，加上直属公安分局以及法轮功学员所在地公安派出所为主力，合计至少一千几百人参与此次抓捕。此次行动，东港市<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多名法轮功学员被抓捕。张伟也遭抓捕和抄家，抢走法轮书籍、资料若干、笔记本电脑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>台、打印机<span lang="EN-US">2</span>台、几部手机。张伟被关进丹东看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，辽宁丹东地区东港市法院对<span lang="EN-US">11</span>名法轮功学员非法庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，东港市法院对法轮功学员下达判决。张伟被非法判重刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，现非法关押在辽宁女子监狱<span lang="EN-US">1</span>监区<span lang="EN-US">7</span>小队。张伟一直坚持炼功，曾多次被打骂、体罚、强制“转化”，张伟曾绝食反迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张卫国</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：江苏省南通市民营企业家，其经营的源景公司与江苏宝泽公司的一起施工合同纠纷案诉讼中败诉。张卫国认为该案败诉系通州区人民法院法官俞妙琴“枉法裁判”所致，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日在本地濠滨论坛发帖，实名举报俞妙琴法官，并留下了自己的姓名、身份证号、手机号、居住地址等信息。此贴点击量暴涨，引起轰动。发帖一个月后，通州区人民法院向公安机关报警。警方以张卫国涉嫌寻衅滋事罪予以刑拘，随后逮捕。检察院提起公诉，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，江苏省南通市海门区人民法院公开审理张卫国被“寻衅滋事”罪。这是第三次公开开庭审理，尚未判决。张卫国利用网络举报法官俞妙琴枉法裁判完全符合《宪法》第<span lang="EN-US">35</span>、<span lang="EN-US">41</span>条规定。被举报人利用公权力对张卫国进行打击报复，与依法治国精神、保护民营企业家政策相悖。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张文斌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">原籍山东、原定今年大学毕业。因<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日在微信实名公开发布“习近平下课”、“共产党下课”视频后，其微信被封杀，后又遭强迫失踪，目前处于失联状态。此前他曾因言获罪被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天。张文斌说，自己挺身而出，武汉肺炎疫情是导火索。而这段矛头指向习近平的视频使他又遭遇了强迫失踪。目前没有进一步的信息。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张文涛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江西南昌市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份，南昌市西湖区公安分局与东湖区公安分局联合，成立了迫害法轮功学员的专案组。他们通过摄像头查找后进行抓捕、抄家，分别于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日逐一抓捕了张莉、江兰英、张文涛、胡水英、陈宝芝。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，江西省南昌市西湖区法院判法轮功学员张文涛<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US"> 2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张五洲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">人权捍卫者、湖北籍、家住广东清远市。张五洲是被关进广州白云区看守所死亡的张六毛的姐姐。张五洲为了给弟弟的不明死亡讨回公道受到打压，开始关注公益和参与一些民主、人权活动。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，广州女律师孙世华在广州荔湾区华林派出所办案时，受到该所民警殴打并遭脱衣检查侮辱。随行的张五洲和梁颂基作为目击者，在网上公开为孙世华作证。广州警方为此报复，以“寻衅滋事罪”抓捕了张五洲和梁颂基。后梁颂基被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半和张五洲<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。张五洲女士于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日当天，前往广州著名风景区白云山，在山上栏杆上打出横幅，上书“勿忘六世，撤回恶法”、“女律师被殴目击证人”等字样，以此纪念<span lang="EN-US">31</span>年前的六四事件，以及反对中共两会刚刚通过的香港国安法的实施。张五洲把该活动拍照及视频发微信朋友圈和其它平台发布后，翌日（<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日）下午<span lang="EN-US">14</span>时<span lang="EN-US">30</span>分，广东清远市公安局清城区分局石角派出所以张五洲“涉嫌扰乱公共秩序”为由将其清远市家中传唤带走，随后被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日来警方又来抄家。后狱中遭受极其残暴的酷刑虐待。张五洲案于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日在清远市清城区法院开庭，未当庭宣判。张五洲在被法院开庭<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月后宣判，以寻衅滋事罪、妨碍公务罪被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，合并执行<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张希明：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市东丽区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日上午九点三十分，天津市东丽区分局警察、国保大队便衣、军粮城派出所警察共十几个人，闯入张希明家中，强行非法抄家，并抓捕了张希明与他母亲刘玉红。当天下午五点，警察把刘玉红放回家，当晚把张希明关押到东丽区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，军粮城派出所两个警察给刘玉红送来张希明被刑事拘留的通知书。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月底被开庭，后获悉被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">张霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">50</span>岁左右，大连市中山区人，原中山区青云小学教师，法轮功学员，良心犯。因信仰法轮功并起诉江泽民，曾被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，被送洗脑班<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日在学校上班时间又被大连市国保与民主广场派出所警方联合绑架抓走，家被查抄，电脑及相关法轮功资料等均被搜走。其丈夫孙俊区派出所问询，已被扣押，后得知夫妇二人均被关押在大连市姚家看守所羁押。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，其被大连中山区检察院以涉嫌“邪教罪”正式批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年被大连市中山区法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”秘密判处<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个月。其不服提起上诉，大连市中级法院未经二审即对她维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月底，张霞被送往辽宁省女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张小麦：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">原名陈煜，浙江临海市基督徒。张小麦</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">(</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈煜）因在开设网上书店“小麦书房”销售基督教书籍</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">,</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月被捕</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">,</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">在张小麦于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月被中共当局以「网上销售非法境外宗教出版物」被捕后，公安部曾通报全国，要求各地国保根据从「小麦书房」搜到的发货订单接触收货人，就其购买书籍的取向和「当地非法宗教活动的情况」进行取证，有上万人被问询。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">27</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日一审判决，以非法经营罪判</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">7</span><span minor-fareast;">年有期徒刑。并处以罚金</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万，所扣押</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12864</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本书予以销毁。判决书同时裁定，被告除了被罚</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万元外，还须追缴售书违法所得的</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万元上缴国库，无法追缴的，由被告退赔，并须予判决生效后十天内缴纳。这是对传播基督教的基督徒的赤裸裸的镇压。刑期至：</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2026</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张小平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">洛阳维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>号，洛阳政府为了修建西环路，在程序不合法的情况下，对张小平家宅基地上的房屋进行了强拆，张小平也因此被逼自学法律，走上了依法维权抗争之路。张小平通过信息公开、行政诉讼等法律途径获取了一些关于修建道路的政府信息，通过对这些信息的分析，发现了前洛阳市市长郭洪昌、李柳身违法修建西环路造成至少<span lang="EN-US">1</span>亿元国有资产流失的事实。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，张小平就这一事实，实名向驻河南中央第一巡视组<span lang="EN-US">65</span>号邮寄了一封《举报信》，此信查询单显示<span lang="EN-US">3.28</span>日已经妥投。巡视组不但没有保护张小平举报人的身份，此举更是将张小平暴露在被举报人的眼皮之下，被打击报复也是迟早之事； 因为举报的事情，张小平接到过威胁电话。关于泄漏举报人信息的问题，张小平通过新浪微博发声质疑，并要求相关部门查处。其最后一个博文发于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，结果，违法人员没得到查处，举报人却被抓了进去。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，洛阳公民张小平疑因举报厅级干部被刑事拘留，其丈夫张智斌行政拘留。原因疑是他们向中央巡视组举报原洛阳市市长郭洪昌、李柳身（正厅级干部）。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，张小平被洛阳公安局南昌路分局（电话<span lang="EN-US">0379-64316110</span>）抓捕；涉嫌罪名是“寻衅滋事”，<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日早被刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被批捕。羁押在洛阳看守所。后无进一步信息。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张小琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">重庆涪陵区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生，女。张小琴<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日在涪陵讲法轮功时被构陷，被涪陵区国保警察抓捕、抄家。抄走电脑、打印机、大法书籍等物品，后被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，张小琴被批捕。被绑架构陷大半年后，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被重庆南川区法院庭审，后悉被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张星姬<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省长春市二道区朝鲜族法轮功学员。千根太、张星姬夫妇在修炼法轮功前，曾在长春市二道区创办食品厂，一九九九年七月中共开始迫害法轮功后，很多法轮功学员进京和平请愿，有的被迫害致流离失所、无家可归。千根太、张星姬夫妇收留几位法轮功学员，被中共发现，后来被迫关闭了食品厂。中共警察上门骚扰不断，千根太、张星姬夫妇不得不将家里的三套房子变卖，被迫流离失所。后遭劳教。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月下旬，千根泰、张星姬夫妇被长春市二道区公安分局和顺街派出所警察抓捕、关押。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月获悉，千根泰、张星姬夫妇被长春市二道区法院枉判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张雪春：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">微信名海燕，维权人士。于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被沈阳市和平分局以（聚众犹乱社会秩序）罪刑拘，目前关押在沈阳市第一看守所，于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日批捕。张雪春家人委托的代理律师向大家征集在北京最高检察院、最高人民法院的目击证人，证明张雪春在按照我国相关法律法规，依法有序向最高人民检察院，最高人民法院，提出司法改革建议过程中，没有任何违法行为，更没有任何犯罪行为以事实，然后走正常法律程序，还当事人以清白，请大家自愿报名，为张雪春出庭作证，证明其当事人无罪。已有上百人目击者报名上庭作证。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张雪莲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">甘肃酒泉市瓜州县法轮功学员。此前，张雪莲因信仰真、善、忍，曾被吉林省长春黑嘴子劳教所劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，被无理剥夺工作，并曾被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，在甘肃女子监狱遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，张雪莲，被国保警察抓捕到敦煌看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，在没有通知家人的情况下，敦煌法院去看守所，宣读对张雪莲的判决结果：<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张艳会：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大午案受害人。<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">2020</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日凌晨，河北大午农牧集团负责人孙大午及其亲属并集团子公司法人等近<span lang="EN-US">30</span>人被警方突击抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">16</span>时，大午案经历<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天庭审后当庭宣判：</span>张艳会<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">被判</span>有期徒刑有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">张永宝</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：辽宁省鞍山市人，法轮功信仰者。因信仰、宣传法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日晚在高俊的七岭子家中，张永宝、高俊、、二人被辽阳公安局警察跟踪绑架、构陷，后经辽阳县法院三次庭审，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日二人被一审以犯“邪教罪”分别冤判有期徒刑。其中，高俊被重判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其不服已提起上诉。张永宝被冤判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张玉红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁阜新市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日晚，张玉红和法轮功学员边春艳、王金凤骑电动自行车外出。在阜新市干休所附近，张玉红、边春艳遭阜新市太平分局国保大队和建设派出所所长于鹏等警察跟踪抓捕，王金凤走脱。当晚边春艳在太平分局挣脱手铐走脱。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，张玉红被太平区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，上诉后被阜新市中法维持原判。</b>同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，张玉红被关押到辽宁女子监狱，分到第<span lang="EN-US">5</span>监区。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月下旬，张玉红被迫害致脑出血，昏迷不醒，住在沈阳<span lang="EN-US">739</span>医院<span lang="EN-US">ICU</span>病房。家属赶到医院，病房已被十多名狱警看守，狱警不准家属接近探视。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 39.95pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张玉莲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省南阳市法轮功学员，年过七旬。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，张玉莲曾两次被判刑，累计陷冤狱七年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>至<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，河南省南阳市公安局统一行动，在南阳地区开始大面积绑架法轮功学员。两陷冤狱的七旬法轮功学员张玉莲老太再被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，张玉莲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个月，勒索罚金五千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张玉明：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1955</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，河北遵化市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，遵化多个村镇的数十名法轮功学员几乎同时在凌晨<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点多遭到警察的入室抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日张玉明被遵化市法院宣判<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">,</span></b>被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">6000</span>元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张展</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：女，<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年代出生，陕西省籍人，上海市浦东新区常驻居民，网络异见人士，公民记者、民主公民。硕士学位，毕业后即在上海谋职工作；因不满中共政府的政治现状，长期在网络平台发布批评“一党专政”、腐败滥权等言论，其做派活跃、内容尖锐而颇具针对性，故而曾多次被上海市警方约谈、传唤及威胁；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年以来，因其在微信等网络平台大量转发香港“反送中”抗议视频及文图资料，尤其是每天自己撰文发声，利用行为艺术等为声援香港举牌，随于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被上海警方传唤，自此失联，后知其被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，其父因受警方威胁，故对外拒透其具体信息；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，终获释放；据悉，羁押期间，其曾被两次做强制性“精神病鉴定”。此前被羁押于上海市浦东新区看守所。张展自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日左右去到武汉报导当地疫情，一直在微信、推特、<span lang="EN-US">YouTube </span>等社交媒体平台上直播武汉的现场情况，并尽其所能地帮助受疫情影响的人维权。张展在武汉实地写了大量关于武汉疫情的真实报道。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日在武汉遭“强迫失踪”，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被上海市浦东分局刑事拘留，被控罪名是寻衅滋事，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月遭正式逮捕。被起诉，其在狱中绝食抗议，身体状况极差。现羁押在浦东新区看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，张展女士案一审开庭，并当庭宣判，张展女士因言获罪被上海浦东新区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张珍华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川达州法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生。四川省万源市茶品公司的退休职工。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日下午，张珍华正在友人毛坤家做客休息，又被成都市金牛区分局国保警察、茶店子派出所孟红等一伙警察疯狂砸门抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点半，被四川省成都市金牛区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张正廷：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省丹东市经济合作开发区访民、台属。张正廷于<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年投资于丹东市振兴区浪头镇的顺达微孔过滤器厂，到<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年，张正廷投资的厂房恰好在丹东市城区公路扩建规划内而需要搬迁。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，地方政府在无任何手续的情况下，出动公安、城管以及社会人员几百号人，对张正廷的顺达过滤器厂层层包围，将厂房夷为平地。张正廷的妻子宋玉洁还被殴打致伤。正是在地方申诉无望的情况下，张正廷、宋玉洁夫妻才不得已进京告御状。想不到，这一告就是<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个年头，且每年的敏感时期都要被维稳，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年十八大前夕，丹东市政府提出给张正廷、宋玉洁夫妇俩<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元维稳补偿费，张正廷拒绝后被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。如此政府却诬陷其为敲诈勒索。张正廷今年已经<span lang="EN-US">76</span>岁，其在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日凌晨零点<span lang="EN-US">48</span>分，被辽宁省丹东市驻京维稳人员<span lang="EN-US">10</span>余人，闯入其位于北京市大兴区的暂住地，强行截回辽宁丹东。后被丹东市经济合作开发区公安分局刑拘，理由是张正廷涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被正式逮捕。羁押在丹东市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张志江：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赤峰市元宝山区五家镇小石头分金桥村居民，法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日晚在大水清道上被喀喇沁旗楼子店派出所警察绑架。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日上午，赤峰元宝山区五家镇村警李文明领着锦山公安局警察闯到张志江家非法抄家，在家里没人的情况下，搜走了大法书。并将张志江非法关押在喀喇沁旗锦山看守所。之后，喀喇沁旗公安局编造材料，将构陷张志江的案卷上报到喀喇沁旗检察院，检察院以张志江炼法轮功、悬挂真相条幅等理由，非法起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，内蒙古赤峰市喀喇沁旗法院开庭非法庭审法轮功学员张志江。张志江为自己做了无罪辩护。法院随后将张志江非法判刑，具体刑期不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">章军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省南充市蓬安县巨龙镇法法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年开始修炼法轮功，曾被中共抓捕、判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被西城派出所警察抓捕、构陷；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被南充市顺庆区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵爱真</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：山东菏泽法轮功学员，女，生于<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年，菏泽市牡丹区糖果食品厂退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日傍晚，王翠英在路边发送真相册子时，被跟踪监控的牡丹区公安局警察抓捕。当日晚上，国保大队警察闯入独居的赵爱真家中，将她抓捕，并抄家，将家中的两台电脑、三台打印机、大法书、真相资料、光盘、打印纸等大量个人物品尽数抄走。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，王翠英、赵爱真两人被牡丹区公安分局刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，遭批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，鄄城县法院下的判决，王翠英被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚款两万元；赵爱真被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款一万五千元。赵爱真刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵晨宇：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">昆明市女教师、法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年五十五岁，原是昆明市第三十中学一级教师，中文系研究生，是一位学生爱戴的好老师。赵晨宇曾于<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。赵晨宇于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初回西双版纳傣族自治州景洪市探望年迈的母亲，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日刚返回到昆明家中，就被跟踪而来的西双版纳景洪市国保大队警察抓捕、抄家。于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日在西双版纳再次被庭审，判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。被关押在西双版纳傣族自治州景洪市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵鄂川：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贵州省贵阳市法轮功学员。赵鄂川<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被警察绑架。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点至<span lang="EN-US">11</span>点半遭贵阳市南明区法院被庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，南明区法院告知律师，对赵鄂川判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。赵鄂川提出上诉。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，律师已经把赵鄂川的上诉状递交到贵阳市中级法院。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><a name="_Hlk54972182"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵根法：</span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk54972182;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵根法、黄春玲、刘洪兰、乔华荣四人都是山东省曲阜市的法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，黄春玲在刘洪兰家做客，赵根法、乔华荣夫妻去看她们，刚坐下还没说几句话，曲阜市国保大队人员就进入刘洪兰家，以「非法集会、集体学法」等罪名，将他们抓捕至书院派出所，另外以「把你的包拿过来看一下」为由将赵根法钥匙夺走，在赵根法、乔华荣夫妻二人都不在场、家中无人的情况下抄家，将法轮功书籍、手机、光盘、笔记本计算机、内存卡、</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk54972182;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">U</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk54972182;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">盘等几十件物品劫走。第二天，即<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，赵根法被关押在曲阜市拘留所；乔华荣、刘洪兰被送往济宁市看守所进行关押；黄春玲被关押在泗水县拘留所。后赵根法、黄春玲、刘洪兰、乔华荣，被抓捕、关押一年多，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日遭济宁市任城区法院庭审，赵根法被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，黄春玲、刘洪兰被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，乔华荣被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。四人都被非法罚款一万元。赵根法刑期至：</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2023</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">赵国江</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：湖北省襄樊市人，襄樊铁路客运段职工，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因信法轮功，早年曾被非法关押拘禁<span lang="EN-US">4</span>次，<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年被冤判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，赵国江被襄阳市樊城法院秘密非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，随后被送湖北省范家台监狱八监区服刑。出狱后，因他继续坚持信仰、宣传法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日又被襄阳樊城区柿铺派出所警方刑拘，家被搜查，被关押在襄阳市第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被襄阳市樊城法院再次以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”枉法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。后被送往襄南监狱，但被拒收，又被送范家台监狱，因体检不合格拒收，现又关押在襄阳市第二看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">赵海军：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1966</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，黑龙江省哈尔滨市人，法轮功学员，在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月因信仰法轮功，并与其妻等人为中共镇压、迫害法轮功到北京和平请愿，被当局抓捕，先被关押于哈尔滨双城市看守所，后又被送到双城区单城敬老院进行强制洗脑教育，期间因屡受虐待酷刑愤而绝食抗议，当局才不得不于<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月将其释放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月因前往北京为法轮功进行和平请愿，而被北京警方抓捕，并被关押于北京市团河劳教所，直至一年多后方予以释放。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日因其屡次控告迫害法轮功的元凶江泽民，遂被当地警方从家中抓走，并被以涉邪教罪刑拘，其家遭查抄。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被双城区检察院转正式批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被哈尔滨双城区法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；其不服上诉，后虽经哈尔滨市中级法院二审，但依然维持原判。目前在黑龙江省呼兰监狱服刑。据悉，因在狱中遭遇虐待，致其长期不能排尿而被强制打针。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">赵海通：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1961</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日出生，青海省海西州人，新疆民主维权公民，中国在押政治犯。因长期致力于为新疆地区弱势群体、维吾尔族群体及政治犯、良心犯等维权呼吁，近年来又南下广东，积极与南方各地维权公民、人权捍卫者等一起参与街头民主运动，举行各种声援举牌和集会活动，故而在所处之地备受民众欢迎；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，曾因前往湖北武汉会见人权活动家秦永敏，惨遭武汉警方的野蛮殴打，差点丧命；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，曾因努力表达维权公民正当合法的诉求，而不惧风险在广州火车站多次举牌，宣传民主理念，“抗议流氓政府打压民主人士”等；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾因参与声援安徽民主人士张林之女张安妮失学事件，而遭警方强行拘押；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，曾因在新疆吐鲁番市帮助维吾尔族公民进行维权，而被新疆警方刑拘，并被关押于新疆乌鲁木齐市六道湾看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，被新疆警方宣布以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，终被新疆维吾尔自治区乌鲁木齐市法院以同罪名秘密重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年。目前在新疆维吾尔自治区塔城市乌苏市乌苏监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵怀国：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">基督徒，湖南省张家界市慈利县常驻居民，慈利县伯特利基督教会建立人，伯利恒教会主任牧师，中国在押良心犯。因笃信基督，而于，<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年起从从东北到湖南省慈利县传福音，同年创办伯特利家庭教会，信徒多以年长者为主；因其所属教会曾多次被官方要求加入“三自教会”，均因价值理念不合而被其及教会众信徒拒绝，遂成为当局排挤、维稳打压的对象；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，曾遭大批公安警方及宗教局人员闯入教会打砸；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，慈利县宗教局曾出动县民族宗教事务局、公安局、城管等部门近<span lang="EN-US">50</span>人，强行撬开伯特利教会大门，毁坏教会用品，撕毁墙上宗教信仰标志，并抄走《圣经》、诗歌本福音单张、钢琴等各类教会用品；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其被张家界市慈利县警方突然以涉嫌’煽动颠覆国家政权罪’刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，被慈利县检察院以同罪名正式批捕，指控其因使用翻墙软件浏览境外媒体有关武汉疫情的报导，又转发嘲讽政府的打油诗等文字，属于严重危害国家安全行为；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其“煽动颠覆国家政权罪” 案在张家界市中级法院开庭受审，公诉方建议量刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>个月，法官称将择日宣判。目前疑被羁押于慈利县看守所（湖南省张家界市慈利县零阳镇，邮政编号：<span lang="EN-US">427200</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，抚顺市新宾县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，赵杰和另一法轮功学员走在路上，被抚顺市新宾县公安局国保大队和派出所警察抓捕，在抚顺市第一看守所被关押迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被辽宁省抚顺市法轮功学员被抚顺市顺城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金两万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川西昌市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日下午，被国安抓捕控制后抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><a name="_Hlk54973417"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵俊香：</span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk54973417;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省庆云县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，山东省庆云县公安局国保大队纠集几十个警察，抓捕了正在学习法轮大法著作的<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多名法轮功学员。根据长期电话监听和监控，警察又抓捕<span lang="EN-US">10</span>余人，共计<span lang="EN-US">46</span>人，其中大多数是<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁以上的老人，大部份法轮功学员被抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日上午，在庆云县法院，夏津县法院人员对六名仍被关押的庆云法轮功学员，赵俊香、王素娟、杜全村、段桂霞、于炳兰、张连云庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，山东夏津县法院开出判决书：赵俊香判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，杜全村判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，王素娟判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，于炳兰判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，张连云判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。赵俊香刑期至：</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2026</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵丽英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川内江法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1947</span>年生，原在四川内江市铁路机务段小学教书，已退休，现居住内江铁路机械学校家属宿舍。在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日下午，赵丽英在内江市区贴法轮功传单，被内江市中区公安分局派人跟踪，抓捕，并抄家，被关押到内江市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，赵丽英被构陷到了内江检察院。之后，家人、朋友一直没有得到任何信息。直到<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月底，赵丽英已经被非押一年多，家人去给她送衣物时，才被看守所人员告知，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，赵丽英被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款二千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员，哈尔滨市轴承厂退休职工，现年已经七十岁了。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日上午，赵林在南岗区先锋路附近粘贴了一张“法轮大法好”不干胶，被南岗公安分局国保警察抓捕、抄家，抢走其家中法轮大法书籍。后获悉被判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵林（河北）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北张家口市桥东区法轮功学员。赵林<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日上午被张家口市公安局桥东分局<span lang="EN-US">51</span>路派出所警察抓捕，并抄走手机维修小店工作用的计算机，同时抄走法轮功资料。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，桥西区法院定对赵林开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月赵林被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵美华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邯郸法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，赵美华被复兴区刑警队和铁路大院派出所警察抓捕，被关押在邯郸第三看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日下午，邯郸市磁县法院对赵美华视频开庭。后得知，赵美华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵明堂：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山西省侯马市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月中旬赵明堂于被判刑四年。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵明堂是<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日左右在侯马市新田广场发真相资料时被警察绑架的，当天晚上被警察赵建林带人非法抄了家。第十天时，赵明堂被非法批捕。十一月中旬在曲沃法院被非法开庭时，赵明堂的儿子与弟弟进入了法庭。开庭中，赵明堂被戴手铐、脚镣，他大声喊“法轮大法好”。赵明堂曾在山西祁县监狱被非法关押七年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵仁霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年生。山东省青岛法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日下午五点左右，赵仁霞从住处下楼，被青岛开发区公安分局国保大队警察绑架，而后把赵转移到户口管辖地灵珠山派出所。<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日下午五点左右，灵珠山派出所警察将赵押到青岛市普东看守所羁押。后遭批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，赵仁霞被青岛市黄岛区法院判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵任远：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广西桂林市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日半夜，谢建新与妻子赵任远被桂林市七星分局的派出所警察声称“测体温”闯入家中，搜查抄走<span lang="EN-US">1</span>轮功书籍、资料、法轮功币等物品，并抓捕、构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被庭审，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日均被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵维凯：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">太原郇城归正基督教会同工。<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年生。他跟教会传道人安彦魁是好搭档。他俩从小就是好友，后来又一起到王怡牧师创办的成都华西神学院读神学，又一起回到太原服侍教会。赵维凯和妻子李鑫有三个孩子，为了不让孩子接受无神论洗脑教育，他们坚持在家教育孩子，因此多次被民宗局、教委、国宝等有关部门上门约谈，以抓捕相威胁强迫他送孩子上公立学校，被赵维凯拒绝。今年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日赵维凯被警察以“宗教诱骗”之名传唤和抄家，他的妻子李鑫也在同一天被传唤。后妻子李鑫获释，但赵维凯却被处以行政拘留约十五天的处罚。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日又被刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被正式批捕。据家属收到的逮捕通知书，大致内容是：经文水县检察院批准，由文水县公安局逮捕，羁押在方山县看守所。罪名是所谓“非法持有宣扬恐怖主义极端主义物品”。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵文静</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵文静、黄金桔、吕月霞、郭春该及张迪<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">为涉</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省商丘巿宁陵县双庙村教会教案成员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日该教会一座兴建中的教堂，遭到数百名政府人员强拆，双方发生争执，教会物品被毁坏，信徒被打伤，数十人包括该<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名负责人被公安带走，后这<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人被拘留。他们被指涉嫌“寻衅滋事”及“非法拘禁”罪，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被县检察院正式逮捕。其中张迪是临近一教会的传道人，为协助该教会建教堂，而遭牵连得。目前，所有被捕者被羁押在宁陵县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，该教会成立<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，信徒百多人，当局曾要求加入三自教会不遂。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵熙茹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈尔滨市道外区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日哈尔滨市松北区公安分局绑架了<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功学员：石香云、贾艳玲、包义、魏续旺、孔庆艳、朱凤英、赵熙茹、刘君、任秀英、杨骐骥、吴樨、张树霞、宫文义。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被松北区检察院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被哈尔滨市松北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵兴有：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江法轮功学员赵兴有，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">79</span>岁，和老伴史桂芝，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年七十七岁，家住黑龙江省哈尔滨市双城区水泉乡。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，双城房产一工作人员去赵兴有夫妇所居住的水泉乡赵家村一村民家，给该村民的房屋拍照，发现赵兴有夫妇家的院墙上喷写有“法轮大法好”的字样，此工作人员心生恶念，把字样拍照下来，传给双城区公安局、六一零。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，警察将赵兴有夫妇抓捕。送哈尔滨做身体检查后，因史桂芝身体不合格，被放回家，赵兴有被劫持到双城看守所，关押六天放回。放回后，指使保人监视他们，不准往墙上写字、不准去炼功点、不准接触修炼人等。后双城公安局警察将赵兴有、史桂芝夫妇构陷到哈尔滨市法院，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，法院法逮捕通知书，水泉乡派出所苏永生等又将赵兴有、史桂芝夫妇再次绑架，赵兴有被劫持到双城看守所非法关押，史桂芝因检查身体不合格放回。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，史桂芝再次被非法抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月上旬，赵兴有被冤判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，史桂芝被冤判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。史桂芝被劫持到黑龙江省女子监狱，赵兴有被劫入哈尔滨市呼兰监狱。赵兴有刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵秀娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: lang="EN-US">4</span>日，刘社红和妻子赵秀娟在荆州市被抓捕，被关押在荆州市荆州区西门看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日获悉，刘社红被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，妻子赵秀娟被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵秀芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江安达市女法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日晚赵秀芝、裴玉凤、陈景捷<span lang="EN-US">3</span>位法轮功学员被警察等非法闯入各自的家中抓捕的。赵秀芝、裴玉凤、陈景捷被关押在安达看守所。后获悉裴玉凤被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半，陈景捷被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半。赵秀芝被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赵颜华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1981</span>年生，系北京首安消防公司工程师。赵颜华于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日上午，被李桥派出所警察抓捕，当晚送往顺义看守所。关押十个月，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被北京市顺义区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索罚金三千元。判决书声称：“本院依法组成合议庭，公开开庭审理了本案。”却不让家人亲属参与旁听。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;
