style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">内蒙古呼伦贝尔市莫力达瓦达斡尔族自治旗（莫旗）法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1958</span>年生。满族，以前在呼伦贝尔市莫旗中心商店工作。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月开始修炼法轮大法。肇淑芝坚持法轮功，遭中共邪党<span lang="EN-US">8</span>次抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次关押、<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次劳教、<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次判刑、<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次洗脑班迫害，死里逃生，夫离女散，被迫流离失所，有家不能回。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，肇淑芝和扎兰屯市法轮功学员任小梅，乘坐由扎兰屯市往返莫旗的大客车，在莫旗客运站被乘警拦截，要求手机扫码、检查身份证，遭到拒绝，之后，他们给公安局打电话，公安警察来了之后，开始给肇淑芝和任小梅照相，直接把她们抓捕到内蒙古阿荣旗看守所非法关押。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，肇淑芝被非法开庭（视频开庭），并被非法勒索两万元人民币。任晓梅被非法勒索两千元。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，任小梅被非法判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，从阿荣旗看守所出来时强迫签字。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月份，肇淑芝被扎兰屯市法院非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，抓捕到内蒙古呼和浩特第<span lang="EN-US">1</span>女子监狱。目前在呼和浩特第<span lang="EN-US">1</span>女子监狱遭受迫害。这是肇淑芝第<span lang="EN-US">9</span>次遭受中共抓捕迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">郑淑春：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生，家住丹东市四道沟胜利街。郑淑春曾于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年被丹东<span lang="EN-US">4</span>道沟派出所警察抓捕，遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，在辽宁女子监狱期间，长时间不让睡觉，被强迫“转化”，但无论监狱用什么酷刑，都没能改变郑淑春的信仰。郑淑春每天被强制最多做<span lang="EN-US">16</span>个小时的奴工，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年的牢狱生活，使她身心受到极大的摧残。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，因张贴真相真相不干胶，被人恶告。下午<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点半左右，遭丹东六道口派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，郑淑春案开庭，家属聘请的律师为她做了无罪辩护。一审被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。郑淑春依法向丹东中级法院上诉。二审改判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年半，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。　<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，郑淑春被丹东看守所劫持辽宁女子监狱<span lang="EN-US">8</span>监区<span lang="EN-US">5</span>小队迫害。狱中遭酷刑迫害，郑淑春瘦得皮包骨。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">钟国权：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年生，身体极度。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日上午，钟国权在黑龙江密山县大街上发真相资料被密山市利民派出所（二所）警察抓捕，后刑事拘留，因身体有病，被取保候审。钟国权于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被密山法院开庭审理，第二天，钟国权被强行送进鸡西看守所。几天后，钟国权家人接到法院非法判决钟国权<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月的判决书。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 10.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp; </span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">钟华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">成都青年法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年代生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，钟华、冉文芳在街上给一个人讲了大法真相，当她们离开后，这个人拨打<span lang="EN-US">110</span>恶意举报，驷马桥派出所通过监控，找到正在回家路上的钟华和冉文芳，将她们抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，钟华和冉文芳被成都金牛区法院判刑，钟华<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金一万，冉文芳<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，罚金六千元。她们上诉后，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，成都市中院法院对她们维持原判。钟华和冉文芳被非法关押在成都郫县看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">钟兴秀：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">江西省武宁县人，法轮功学员，在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年期间，曾因组织、参与制作、印刷法轮功宣传光盘、书刊等行动，传授打印、刻录、装订技术等，而遭到地方当局严密监控和打击。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，在与他人搬运、携带<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年神韵晚会光盘、《明慧周刊》等相关海外法轮功影像杂志资料时，被武宁县警方获悉，当场拘捕，其家被抄。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其被江西省武宁县人民法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，经九江市中级人民法院二审依然驳回起诉，维持原判。目前被羁押于江西省武宁县看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">钟义芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生，攀枝花市攀钢集团公司第二机械厂退休工人，法轮功学员。自从中共开始迫害法轮功后，钟义芳非法劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年钟义芳被判刑八年，于<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被关押到四川省龙泉驿女子监狱。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月才出狱回家<span lang="EN-US">.2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月又遭中共当局抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月获悉，钟义芳被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半。她现在被迫害得出现严重的尿毒症，骨瘦如柴，肚子肿的老大，每天看守所给她打针。生命健康令人担忧。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">仲周（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年出生，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州人，又叫“尊珠”，阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县格尔登寺僧人，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，因其协助侄子兼徒弟、同寺僧人彭措（又叫平措，已于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日自焚死亡，时年<span lang="EN-US">20</span>岁）为纪念中共当局镇压拉萨<span lang="EN-US">3</span>•<span lang="EN-US">14</span>事件三周年，抗议中共政府对藏人的强权高压统治，以自焚方式（指一种藏人抗议暴政、伸张正义的方式，即藏人自焚者把自己整个奉献出来，以清晰的理智、自愿的心态和惨烈的方式向暴政表达最强烈抗议的无奈选择，以期使公众舆论对极权和高压统治者予以最强烈的谴责或改变对手的情感）在阿坝县城洽唐中街实施自焚行动；同时，因其担心当局野蛮抢夺自焚尸体，而将自焚后的彭措转移隐藏到格尔登寺内，由此引发中共军警与当地僧人、藏人的激烈对抗和冲突；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，其随被阿坝藏族羌族自治州马尔康县警方抓捕，并被以“安排转移、藏匿彭措达<span lang="EN-US">11</span>个小时之久，导致彭措因为体表大面积烧伤、延误救治而死亡”为罪由刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被四川省马尔康县法院以“故意杀人罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。目前服刑监狱不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周嫦兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月出生，家住广州市白云区。周嫦兰（周常兰）因正义销毁白云区景泰北社区多次出现的诽谤、诬陷法轮功的邪恶宣传栏，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，在白云区景泰街云苑南禁毒广场，被白云区公安分局和白云区景泰派出所警察抓捕，被关押到白云区看守所。直到<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，才得知周嫦兰被秘密关押、判刑的消息。周嫦兰被荔湾区检察院起诉，遭荔湾区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周德元</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：长沙市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁，家住在长沙市左家塘附近的烟草公司宿舍。从一九九八年，周德元开始修炼法轮功。她是一位开朗的常德人，用湖南人都能听懂的常德话和人们交流。从常德市轴承厂退休后，她与家人迁居到了长沙。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，周德元被抓捕，十五天行政拘留结束，又被关押在长沙市第四看守所。后，周德元被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被转送至湖南省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周殿文</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：黑龙江省哈尔滨市依兰县法轮功学员。男，七十多岁，原中煤黑龙江省依兰县达连河煤矿退休工人，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月份发法轮功台历时，被人诬告，被依兰县公安局国保大队队长杨维兴带人抓捕到看守所。周殿文老人，被关押一年多，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年末被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，目前在黑龙江省泰来监狱遭受关押迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周海燕：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁大连法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，大连公安局国保支队同大连开发区公安分局属下五彩城派出所、湾里派出所、黄海路派出所、海青派出所、董家沟派出所等出动数十个警察，以拦路抓捕、抢劫、入室抢劫的方式在多个地点同时实施多起抓捕法轮功学员案。十名当时被抓捕的法轮功学员被非法批捕：周海燕、胡志琴（女，五十八岁）、来桂芳（女，四十二岁）、时宁瑶（女，三十八岁）、方芳（女，五十四岁）、林景萍（女，四十六岁）、贾秀春（女，四十一岁）、曹娥（女，五十五岁）、武丽艳（女，五十二岁）和刘淑芬（女，七十八岁）。八十一岁的郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被取保候审。后<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月八名法轮功学员被大连开发区法院判刑：周海燕<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，胡志琴<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，来桂芳<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，时宁瑶<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，林景萍<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，方芳<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，贾秀春<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。周海燕刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周金莲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南省郴州市永兴县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十一岁的周金莲是永兴县的一个普通家庭妇女，家住湖南省郴州市永兴县沙子光。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，周金莲在永兴县鲤鱼塘镇向民众讲述法轮功真相，被鲤鱼塘派出所的警察抓捕，之后被关押在郴州市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月下旬，周金莲被永兴县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">周克铭：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>出生。黑龙江鸡西市法轮功学员。鸡西市法轮功学员周克铭在发放法轮功资料时，被人诬告。鸡西市公安局鸡冠区公安分局国保、永昌派出所、铁西派出所采取跟踪、监控手段，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日抓捕了包万明、滕淑丽、周克铭。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，包万明、滕淑丽、周克铭被非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人被非法关押在鸡西市看守所<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。包万明、周克铭、滕淑丽，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日遭鸡东法院以视频的方式开庭，近日得知，包万明被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年、罚金十万元；滕淑丽被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>万元；周克铭被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元。周克铭刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周娜：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西太原市万柏林区法轮功学员。周绍山、高继萍夫妻与女儿周娜<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被警察绑架、抄家，在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月左右，周绍山被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元，高继萍被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元，周娜被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周启良：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">周启良、王传煌、汪黎明三人均系江西省武宁县人，法轮功学员，在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年期间，曾因组织、参与制作、印刷法轮功宣传光盘、书刊等行动，学习、传授打印、刻录、装订等技术，使用具有自动拨号及语音功能的手机给他人打电话等，而遭到地方当局严密监控和打击。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，在共同搬运、携带<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年神韵晚会光盘、《明慧周刊》等相关海外法轮功影像杂志资料时，被武宁县警方获悉，当场拘捕，其家分别被抄。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人均被江西省武宁县人民法院一审以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。其三人均表不服，提起上诉，同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，经九江市中级人民法院二审依然驳回起诉，维持原判。目前都被羁押于江西省武宁县看守所。分别刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贵阳市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年生。一人独居在贵阳云岩区省政府大院，她父亲是贵州省政府一名老干部。周琴毕业于贵州大学外语学院，后在贵州省教育学院任教，是一名大学英语教师；由于大学期间的一次事故，摔断脚踝造成残疾。周琴<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年以前就修炼法轮功。周琴<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月遭当局抓捕，家人不知。后表姐和友人们多方查询，在离贵阳市很远的“贵阳市三江女子看守所”查到周琴被关押里面。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日周琴被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，周琴的家人近期收到法院判决书。据说周琴被关押在贵阳羊艾第一女子监狱。因为疫情，家人还没有见到周琴。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周绍山：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西太原市万柏林区法轮功学员。周绍山、高继萍夫妻与女儿周娜<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被警察绑架、抄家，在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月左右，周绍山被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元，高继萍被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元，周娜被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">周世峰：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1964</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，河南省安阳县人，北京锋锐律师事务所主任，<span lang="EN-US"> 2009</span>年度、<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年度“社会公益法律服务先进个人”、<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年中国法律援助“优秀援助律师”、<span lang="EN-US"> 2009-2011</span>年度“北京优秀律师”，知名人权律师。自<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年执业以来，曾代理过多起著名的受害人案件，并于<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月创立北京锋锐律师事务所，广纳包括王宇、刘晓原、王全章等在内的著名人权律师。<span lang="EN-US"> 2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被北京市警方以“严重扰乱社会秩序”、“教唆、组织、策划、资助他人炒作所谓敏感案件” 等为罪由抓走刑拘，其锋锐律师事务所及其办公室被查抄。被指定居所监视居住，其锋锐律师事务所及其办公室被查抄；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被天津市警方以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，被天津市第二中级法院以同罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。现羁押在天津市第一看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周维林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">安徽合肥人权捍卫者、工伤致残人士。周维林<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日出生，原安徽省拖拉机厂退休职工，维权网信息员，安徽省维权人士，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年曹顺利人权捍卫者奖获得者。曾于<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日因工受伤，成为丧失劳动能力的伤残人员，但原所在单位一直不给于办理伤残认定和退休等手续，自此走上维权之路。自<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年起，尤其是<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年期间，因长期坚持实名报导安徽及全国各地多种公权力违法侵权事件，并成为“维权网”信息员，而招致当局的强烈不满和忌恨，曾先后<span lang="EN-US">5</span>次被合肥警方处以行政拘留，并且多次被警方抄家、传唤、威胁甚至殴打。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，各地维权人士发起声援“安妮失学事件”的活动，周维林因前往进行实时报导，而被合肥警方于<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日强行带走，处以行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，又因参与合肥网友聚餐纪念<span lang="EN-US">64</span>活动，遭到警方的报复性拘留，之后获释；但时至<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，合肥警方再次因<span lang="EN-US">64</span>纪念活动而以“涉嫌虚构事实扰乱公共秩序”事由对其进行传唤，并处以行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，合肥警方第三次以参与声援安妮失学事件，维护安妮受教育权活动为由，将其与张林、李化平、姚诚等维权人士一同拘捕，并以涉嫌“聚众扰乱公共场所秩序罪”而刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被当地检察院以同罪名正式批捕，之后被安徽省合肥市地方法院以“聚众扰乱公共场所秩序罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，刑满获释。出狱后仍然在一直坚持为劳工和残疾人维权。周维林于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被合肥市公安局瑶海分局城东派出所（电话：<span lang="EN-US">0551-64483496</span>）秘密抓走了。后获悉遭刑事拘留、逮捕。周维林案已于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日在合肥开庭审理，未当庭宣判。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周喜云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郑州市法轮功学员。女，四十多岁。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日下午，周喜云在荆建秋家中做客，她俩一起被荥阳广武派出所警察、荥阳国保大队警察抓捕，被关押在郑州第三看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，在中原区法院南办公区被开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月下旬，荆建秋和周喜云被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，罚款三万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周向阳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">天津法轮功学员。周向阳从北方交通大学毕业后，分配到天津铁道第三勘探设计院工经处，因工作出色，单位送他到天津大学，又获得投资经济学位；<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>考取了全国首批造价工程师职业资格，成为当时全国仅有的六十位造价工程师之一。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，期间遭受无数酷刑：被彻夜电击至遍体鳞伤、连续三十天熬夜、多次关小号、野蛮灌食等等。周向阳在<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被绑架后，于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，后到天津市滨海监狱原五监区二分监区（现六监区）服刑，一直绝食抵制迫害。一开始，狱警安排六个包夹人（监狱安排的专门负责看管法轮功学员的刑事罪犯人）白天晚上轮流看管周向阳，每天包夹人用担架抬着周向阳去监狱的医院灌食三次。据包夹人说：“有一次给周向阳灌食，包夹人按着他的胳膊和双腿，监狱医院的人强行把胃管从周向阳的嘴里插进去，灌完食之后，周向阳自己把胃管拔出来，管子上面沾满了鲜血。”妻子李珊珊因坚持为丈夫申冤，曾遭到监狱的报复，两次被非法劳教共计三年多。二零一三年劳教制度解体了，李珊珊是从石家庄女子劳教所走出来的最后一个。一家人团聚的日子没有多久。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日早晨七点，天津警察再一次破门而入，把周向阳和妻子李珊珊抓走了。周向阳被冤判七年，李珊珊被冤判六年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周兴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">大连市金州区石河镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日晚，谷秀华（女）、刘希永（男）、周兴（男）、李天学（男）、王丽志（女）、张三曼（女）、谭春荣（女）、孙宝英（女）、刘井龙（男），去大连市金普新区炮台镇袁屯村发放新书《共产主义的终极目的》，被炮台镇派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日下午二在大连市金州法院庭审。后谷秀华、周兴、王丽志，被大连市金州法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；张三曼、谭春荣被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，李天学被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，刘希永、孙宝英、刘井龙的情况还不清楚。周兴刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周妍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">46</span>岁，黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员。哈尔滨市哈尔滨市依兰县公安局<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午对依兰县、佳木斯市桦川县两地法轮功学员实施绑架，到<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日共有<span lang="EN-US">29</span>人被绑架，其中十四名法轮功学员宋玉芝、施凤香、施凤兰、王云杰、周妍、邓术梅、宋孔华、武桂琴、卜宝玲、夏桂华、唐立飞、姚怀英、康艳玲、庞秀贤，与薛宏亮（未修炼法轮功）被长期关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日遭依兰县法院庭审。周研被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年， 处罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周艳波：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">大连市金州区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，周艳波毕业于大连医科大学附属卫校，由国家统一分配到大连开发区医院工作，从事临床护理工作。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年，周艳波开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，没有经过任何法律程序，周艳波被劫持到了马三家劳教所，被劳教两年。遭酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，被国保警察抓捕后，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被视频非法开庭，周艳波被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。目前，周艳波仍被非法关押在大连姚家看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周永杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省农安县法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年生，家住长春市农安县，常在长春市打工。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，周永杰被长春市朝阳区宽平派出所抓捕。关押在长春市第四看守所。此后家属未得到任何信息。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年底，周永杰被关押在长春市女子监狱后，家属才得知，她被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周永林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁锦州凌海市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁。在中共对法轮功的迫害中，孙继萍与丈夫周永林被中共绑架、关押，劳教，在派出所、看守所、劳教所遭酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，孙继萍与丈夫周永林在盘锦市锦采新区大集上告诉人们“法轮大法好”时，被凌海市公安局闫家镇派出所警察绑架，被隔离二十一天后（<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日），孙继萍被非法关押到锦州市女子看守所，周永林被非法关押到凌海市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，凌海市法院对孙继萍与丈夫周永林每人各判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、罚金各一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周玉香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东平度市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>岁生，是平度大泽山镇尹家村一位普通的农村妇女。周玉香<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日与外甥女周君、好友展中香一起到平度仁兆赶集，被仁兆派出所警察抓捕并被刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日上午，周玉香被青岛市黄岛区法院在即墨市普东看守所，通过视频非法庭审，律师做了有理有据的无罪辩护，最后，周玉香被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周远志：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周远志（笔名华梁兴、曾仁全）<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日生。是一名自由撰稿人、独立中文笔会会员，由于长期撰写、发表关于各类社会问题及揭露官员腐败的文章，在<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被湖北省钟祥市国家安全局以“涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权罪”抓捕，获释后周远志在家长期被当局监视居住。根据独立中文笔会的网页显示，他以笔名曾仁全发表多篇敏感文章，其中题目包括“农民以特殊方式表达对江泽民的憎恶”及“人民的名义远离普世价值”。周远志被<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被以“织非法聚集罪”刑事拘留。此前，周远志被指组织访民上访而被当局关押，，被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天原本应于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日释放，但未获释放，随后，被确认其在<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日即遭湖北荆门市公安局东宝分局以“织非法聚集罪”刑事拘留。其妻子张中凤说由于他一向身体不好，她非常担心丈夫的情况。现羁押在荆门市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日在荆门掇刀法院开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日以“组织非法聚集罪判刑期<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，网上寻衅滋事罪<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，诽谤罪<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，决定合并执行<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年零<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月”，刑期<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。目前关押地址：<a name="_Hlk52057464">湖北省荆门市东宝区牌楼镇荆门看守所，电话<span lang="EN-US">0724-8882273</span>，邮编<span lang="EN-US">448121<o:p></o:p></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52057464;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">周育琴</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52057464;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：广东省惠东县人，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因信仰、宣传法轮功，周育琴与石雪梅、刘庆强三人，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被惠东县政法委、<span lang="EN-US">610</span>办及国保等警方非法抓捕，后于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被广东省惠州市惠东县法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”秘密宣判。其中，周育琴被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，并处罚金五万元<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">（刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日</b>）；石雪梅被冤判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元（刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日）；刘庆强被冤判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元（刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日）。三人均不服审判，已向广东省惠州市中级法院提出上诉。</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">目前被关押在惠东县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周再强：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南长沙网民。职业货车司机。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月网上发言支持香港反送中的光复香港、时代革命运动被刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，周再强的亲友才在微信发出消息称：长沙公民周再强近期因在推特上发言支持香港反送中运动而被当局突然抓捕，并以寻衅滋事的罪名刑事拘留，目前已经确认被关押于长沙市第一看守所。据了解，周再强有两个匿名推特号，已持续发推三万多条。香港反送中运动爆发后，他一直都非常关注，也自发和转发了很多推文表示关注和支持。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">朱承志：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">人权捍卫者。朱承志早年与友人合资在云南经营锰矿场，其后被新加入的拍档施计夺去矿场，而对方更抢先入禀法院状告朱承志侵吞矿场。结果，朱承志被判败诉，多年资产化为乌有。他多次向公安厅投诉均不获受理，只好进京上访，却遭关押<span lang="EN-US">40</span>天。朱承志遂在网上组织民间维权运动，包括声援“福州三网友”案。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，他又冒险到医院探望近乎失聪失明的同乡兼同窗“六四铁汉”李旺阳，并协助香港媒体为李作生前唯一一次专访。由于他拒绝在“不再关注李旺阳死亡事件保证书”上签字，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被湖南省公安厅以“扰乱社会治安”之名拘留；其家人于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日收到朱承志的逮捕通知书，指朱承志被省公安控以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”。后获释。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月与谭作人、艾晓明共同荣获中国民主教育基金会颁发的<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年度杰出民主人士奖。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日因祭奠林昭后已遭强迫失踪，后获知其被控“寻衅滋事”而被指定居所监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，林昭祭日当天，朱承志另外<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名维权人士，成功到达苏州灵岩山林昭墓前祭奠。随后，大批警察当场把<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人带走，当中<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人后来获释，但朱承志却和外界失去联系。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日上午，苏州市吴中区法院以寻衅滋事罪名宣判著名人权捍卫者朱承志朱承志<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">朱凤英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈尔滨市道外区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日哈尔滨市松北区公安分局绑架了<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功学员：石香云、贾艳玲、包义、魏续旺、孔庆艳、朱凤英、赵熙茹、刘君、任秀英、杨骐骥、吴樨、张树霞、宫文义。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被松北区检察院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被哈尔滨市松北区被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">朱桂贞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">山东泰安市法轮功信徒，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">64</span>岁的老太太，原泰安市木器厂退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日下午，朱桂贞和平秀英为了让民众了解法轮大法，在邱家店镇某村，发送法轮功资料，并向路人讲述法轮功受迫害的真相，遭邱家店派出所警察绑架，被关到泰安市看守所。后于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，朱桂贞因修炼法轮功，向百姓传播法轮大法，被泰安市泰山区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱海燕：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宁夏银川市永宁县法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1977</span>年生。大学本科毕业，原宁夏银川市永宁县环境监测中心工作人员，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年底开始修炼法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功，朱海燕多次被抓捕、被关押、劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，朱海燕等<span lang="EN-US">14</span>名法轮功学员被银川市永宁县公安局恶警抓捕、抄家，朱海燕被关押在银川市看守所，后被银川市永宁县公安局构陷到银川市西夏区检察院；遭银川市永宁县公安局和银川市西夏区检察院相互勾结迫害。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被银川市西夏区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">朱惠来：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">广东省湛江市人，广东省湛江市东海岛东山镇调青北园村村民，抗强拆维权者，民间誉名“东海岛英雄”，中国在押维权人士。自<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年以来，广东省湛江市政府以“湛江钢铁基地”为名，在无任何批文的前提下（注：该批文直至<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日才拿到，总值人民币<span lang="EN-US">700</span>亿），烂用公权，派出大批警力对该区域东海岛东简镇衔头村、迈奴村、蓄昌村等八条村以及东山镇北园村等一万多名村民进行暴力拆迁，致使万民怨声载道；因之前朱惠来父子一家不愿意为强拆签字，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，湛江市开发区官员随带领数十人，在没有支付拆迁款的情况下，强毁其田地和家园里的果树、帐棚和农作物等；其子朱培忍开车回来，看到父亲被警方殴打，随前往和其一起与警方、强拆官员发生激烈对抗，最终导致<span lang="EN-US">1</span>死多伤（其中致当地治安大队副队长死亡）；随后，其立即被警方刑拘和逮捕，但却被民间誉为“东海岛英雄”。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被广东省湛江市赤坎区中级法院以“故意杀人罪”、“故意伤害罪”一审判处死刑；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，经湛江市赤坎区中级法院二审，改判死缓；其不服，继续上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，广东省高级法院对其案以“事实不清、证据不足”为由“撤销原判、发还重审”；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，广东省湛江市中级法院再次重审朱惠来父子抗强拆杀官员案，仍判死刑。　<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，广东高院（<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>）粤刑终<span lang="EN-US">298</span>号判决书作出终审判决：朱惠来犯故意杀人罪、故意伤害罪，决定执行死刑，缓期二年执行，剥夺政治权利终身，并限制减刑。目前被羁押地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">朱家彩：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贵州毕节威宁县法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十多岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，因发放法轮功资料挂横幅，朱家彩、罗翠琴遭抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日在毕节七星关区法院被庭审，后得知朱家彩被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚款二万元、罗翠琴被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，勒索罚款一万元。朱家彩刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">朱培忍</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：广东省湛江市人，广东湛江东海岛东山镇调青北园村村民，“东海岛英雄”，抗暴维权者。自<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年以来，广东省湛江市政府以“湛江钢铁基地”为名，在无任何批文的前提下（注：该批文直至<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日才拿到，总值人民币<span lang="EN-US">700</span>亿），烂用公权，派出大批警力对该区域东海岛东简镇衔头村、迈奴村、蓄昌村等八条村以及东山镇北园村等一万多名村民进行暴力拆迁，致使万民怨声载道；因之前朱培忍和其父一家不愿意为强拆签字，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，湛江市开发区官员随带领数十人，在没有支付拆迁款的情况下，强毁其父田地和家园里的果树、帐棚和农作物等，其父被严重殴打；其开车回来，看到父亲被警方殴打，随上前与父亲一起与警方、强拆官员发生激烈对抗，最终导致<span lang="EN-US">1</span>死多伤，其随被警方拘捕，但被民间誉为“东海岛英雄”。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其被广东省湛江市赤坎区中级法院以“故意杀人罪”、“故意伤害罪”一审判处死缓。其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月经湛江市赤坎区中级法院二审，改判为无期徒刑。其依然不服，继续上诉，至<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，广东省高级法院对其案以“事实不清、证据不足”为由“撤销原判、发还重审”。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日湛江市中级法院再审朱惠来父子抗暴杀官案，仍为无期徒刑。目前被关押地点不详。其在看守所惨遭酷刑，肝部被打裂，生殖器被打烂，牙齿被打掉，为此曾被送医院抢救。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱素荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年生，家住河北保定蠡县鲍墟乡东孟尝村，在中孟尝小学任教。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，正在学校上课的朱素荣，突然被鲍墟乡派出所警察骚扰，他们并尾随至家中抄家捕人，当天朱素荣就被送至保定看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月二<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被高阳法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月、勒索罚金五万元，朱素荣已上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱宇飙：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1971</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月出生，广东省人，原广州地铁小额贷款有限公司职员，原广东金粤律师事务所、广州市广大律师事务所、广东恒益律师事务所执业律师，广东省第一个公开为法轮功信仰者作无罪辩护的正义律师，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。学生时代，曾就读于广东省中山大学法学专业；法学硕士毕业后，先后曾就职于广东金粤律师事务所、广州市广大律师事务所和广东恒益律师事务所，作执业律师；因为经常热心为弱势群体当事人作代理辩护律师，并以低价或折价收费，甚至不计报酬，所以深受社会大众及业界同仁称许、好评；但因其练习和信仰法轮功而屡遭政府打压逼迫，遂被迫多次转换律所，直至最终其律师执业证被广东司法当局吊销；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年，曾分别为三名法轮功信仰者做无罪辩护，因其法庭辩护词精彩绝伦，堪称经典，顿令中共法庭大为震惊和难堪，随后即被广东司法当局称为“反革命”，将其列为广东省公安厅要维稳严控的“头号人物”；<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其突然被广州市警方野蛮抓捕，后被枉法处劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，送广州市第三劳教所关押；关押期间，曾遭多次酷刑折磨，如“坐老虎凳”、“架飞机”、用湿毛巾盖脸窒息、水淹、在冷天灌凉水、鞭打手指及脚趾、不准睡觉，等等；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，劳教释放后，因其律师证被广州当局故意拖延办理，对其工作和日常生活造成极大不便；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其第二次被广州市海珠区新港派出所警方莫名抓捕、刑拘，家遭查抄，后被广州市海珠区法院以“利用邪教破坏法律实施罪”枉法判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，并送广东省北江监狱服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，虽是其刑满获释日，但又被转送到广东省三水洗脑班非法关押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，再次被广州市海珠区警方十余人闯入抄家，搜走几本其个人阅读的法轮功书籍之后，随即将其绑架到一不知名的法轮功洗脑班关押；据悉，自其被抓至今，家人一直无法知其更多信息。目前被羁押地点不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱兆水：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省舒兰市吉舒镇法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生。一九九八年开始修炼法轮功。曾被非法劳教一年多。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日晚被当地警方抓捕、关押；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月中旬获悉，朱兆水被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">祝亚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">武汉市黄陂区法轮功学员，祝亚是个残疾人，家住武汉市黄陂区前川街，丈夫早逝，她与女儿相依为命。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，祝亚去买菜，被便衣警察拦截。这次抓捕祝亚是由省城“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”亲自操控、指使的，他们闯进家中抄家。武汉市黄陂区法院<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日庭审，被秘密枉判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">珠扎（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">现年<span lang="EN-US">50</span>岁，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县求吉玛乡索日玛村人，原格尔登寺僧人，藏族人权捍卫者、政治犯。因政治诉求，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年曾被当局以不详政治罪名抓捕、判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被警方以涉嫌“组织阿坝民众举办达赖喇嘛<span lang="EN-US">80</span>岁寿辰活动”为罪由，从其僧舍强行带走，自此失联，后从非官方渠道打听得知，其已被正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。据悉，当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 119.25pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">珠玛别克<span lang="EN-US">.</span>穆汗（哈萨克）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">42</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">岁，新疆阿尔泰市人，阿尔泰市喀拉希力克乡武装部官员，哈萨克族政治犯。曾因被新疆中共当局指控在聊天工具微信“乱说话”，“泄漏中共党内机密”，而于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被阿尔泰市警方刑拘、逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，获悉近期已被新疆阿尔泰市法院以“泄露国家机密罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年。据称，其原本在上海读大学的儿子因父亲被判刑，竟遭株连，被校方勒令退学，现已回到新疆家中。其妻子古丽加丽拉也因受牵连，原本在乡政府卫生院工作，也因此被辞退，他本人在银行的<span lang="EN-US">60</span>万元人民币积蓄遭罚没，家里的<span lang="EN-US">50</span>头牛也被政府没收。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">庄友布：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">42</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">岁，福建省宁德市福鼎县人，法轮功学员。曾因信法轮功并参与网上法轮功信息资料接受、传送、现金转帐及宣传等活动，而被宁德市国保人员长期跟踪、蹲点监控。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬，与肖传雄、金丽燕、陈星光、杨贵媚、杨雄、陈开奇，林丽芳、王田等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人先后被宁德市警方抓捕，各人家庭均被查抄，至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，庄友布被宁德市检察院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”正式批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被福建省宁德市蕉城区法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”分别非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>—<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不等，其中，庄友布被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。目前都被关押于福建省宁德市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邹华兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，今年<span lang="EN-US">1951</span>年生，重庆长寿区法轮功学员，原重庆长寿农机公司退休职工，邹华兰因修炼法轮功曾多次遭受迫害：<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次劳教，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次判刑，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次被关洗脑班，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次关押在看守所将近<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，中共政法委书记郭声琨到重庆开会，要求对跨区域活动的维权人士、法轮功学员等要重点打击。重庆市长寿区<span lang="EN-US">610</span>和国保为了完成所谓的“政治任务”，也为了捞取升官资本，开始寻找他们的下手目标。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，邹华兰在贵州结束冤狱回家。因为这段被外省判刑的经历，邹华兰成了长寿区<span lang="EN-US">610</span>和国保的迫害对象。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日左右，长寿区国保支队指使晏家街道派出所警察，到贵州去调查邹华兰被构陷的案子，作为再次迫害的“证据”。然后，又以监控摄像头摄到邹华兰在晏家街道发台历为借口，晏家派出所几个警察，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">33</span>日，闯入邹华兰家中，把邹华兰抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，邹华兰被逮捕，后被关押在长寿区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，邹华兰被重庆市江北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邹佩霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东东营法轮功学员。耿录堂、邹佩霞老夫妻，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年已年过七旬，家住东营市胜利油田孤岛采油厂芙蓉小区。修炼大法前，夫妻俩身体很不好，耿录堂还患有高血压等疾病。一九九六年前后，老俩口修炼法轮大法。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，老俩口去河口地区赶集，向人宣传法轮功，遭人恶告，东营市河口区国保大队下属的义和镇派出所警察，于当天抓捕了夫妇俩。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月开庭，后耿录堂、邹佩霞夫妇均被东营市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，并被勒索罚款三万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">左洪涛</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：秦皇岛市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，秦皇岛市山海关公安分局在左洪涛、崔秋荣夫妇开的“佳合中介”抓捕了夫妻二人及吴文章、杨晓勇、袁素静及李国爱等五名法轮功学员，抄查中野蛮地抢劫了中介周转资金十余万元现金及电动车一辆和其它办公用品。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，山海关区检察院侦监科科长陈铁忠对左洪涛、崔秋荣等人以莫须有的罪名非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，昌黎县法院对四名法轮功学员左洪涛、刘长富、吴文章、李国爱与左洪涛的妻子崔秋荣（不炼功）五人开庭。后判处左洪涛<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年有期徒刑，吴文章<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，李国爱<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刘长富<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，左洪涛妻子崔秋荣（没炼功）<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年零几个月（已获释）。左洪涛刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">结束语：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告是一份月度动态报告，这是第<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">70</span></b>期，肯定仍然会有遗漏和信息滞后的情况。希望大陆各地的人权捍卫者积极补充，请将符合本报告标准而未统计人员情况、以及本报告名单人员的最新情况提供给我们，以便使以后的报告更加翔实和完善。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">维权网联系方法：<span lang="EN-US">wqw2011@gmail.com</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">曹建山、曹瑞平、柴英芝、陈桂荣、邓力平<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">迪娜<span lang="EN-US">.</span>依根别尔德、范路杰、高小平、韩雪松、何菊英、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">胡功、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span>胡水英、黄信、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span>兰桂媛、勒智多杰（藏）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李常秋、</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李春华、</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span
