style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">罗丽、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span>钱风林、全世欣、任秀英、石桂尊、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">沈爱斌、</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">汤菊章、王健、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span>王建华、王莉、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王永生、吴娟、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span></span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吴伟明、</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">翟国兴、张圣相、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵帮海、郑旭飞、</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">周显蓉、靳凤羽、</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、曹建山<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日出生，职业：工人。江苏省南通市崇川区公民。家住江苏省南通市崇川区光明西村。中共官方消息称：“北京时间<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，中国江苏盐城市响水县江苏天嘉宜化工有限公司工厂厂区内发生爆炸事故。截至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日<span lang="EN-US">12</span>时，事故已造成<span lang="EN-US">78</span>人死亡。共有伤员<span lang="EN-US">566</span>人，其中危重伤员<span lang="EN-US">13</span>人，重症<span lang="EN-US">66</span>人。” 随后，对这一重大灾难事故，曹建山申请江苏响水爆炸信息公开。曹建山这一公民行动竟然遭到江苏当局报复，随后南通警方竟然以涉嫌诽谤罪将其刑事拘留。后被监视居住，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月后获取保，但至今仍被禁言。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、曹瑞平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北辛集市马庄乡枣营村维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">30</span>年前因实行计划生育政策，曹瑞平被做结扎手术，但手术做坏了。手术后曹瑞平身体感到非常不适，妇科病增加，时时伴有小腹痛，双腿静脉曲张，导致现在小腿比大腿还粗，肿痛行走不便。向相关部门反映均无人管，自此曹瑞平走上了上访之路。由于上访时常往外跑，不幸家中两个女儿被人强奸，其中有一人是政府官员，现此官员仍在工作岗位上工作，并未得到制裁。曹瑞平丈夫在一连串灾难来临后，抑郁而终。曹瑞平于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日去天安门被带到马家楼，当天晚上无人接，自已从马家楼离开。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日上午到北京国家计生委和民政部投诉无果，无奈于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日连续去天安门，后被送至马家楼，最后由辛集市马庄派出所押回并刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，曹瑞平被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留于石家庄市第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日对曹瑞平实施逮捕。后案件讯息全无，情况不详。后获悉，已释放。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">3</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、柴英芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北省唐山市路北区人，因为在她和前夫董文奖的离婚官司中，董文奖和他表亲陈振朝联合买通异地汉沽区的法官造假判决转移资产，致柴英芝胜诉后没有分得本该分得的资产，被逼于<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年开始上访。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，柴英芝与河北访民曹连生偷渡至台湾金门被抓，于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被台湾移民署遣送回国，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日分别回家。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日下午，柴英芝去国家信访局上访，被唐山市路北区公安局以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，之后被以同罪名逮捕。现关押于唐山市第一看守所。后案件音信全无。后获悉，已释放。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">4</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、陈桂荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">大连瓦房店法轮功学员陈桂荣、陈利荣姐妹俩，在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日与法轮功学员王永生配合发放真相资料时，遭恶意举报被抓捕，被瓦房店法院非法开庭并判刑，姐姐陈桂荣遭诬判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，妹妹陈利荣遭诬判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。陈桂荣刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">5</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、邓力平</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：重庆市渝北区法轮功学员，一九九七年三月二十九日开始修炼法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年已<span lang="EN-US">77</span>岁退休工程师、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，邓力平老先生被重庆市南岸区公安分局秘密关押在市南岸区看守所。后获悉，邓力平在今年初被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，被关押在永川监狱迫害。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">6</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、迪娜<span lang="EN-US">.</span>依根别尔德：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁市人，伊犁市塔城地区鹤峰县居民，哈萨克族，新疆艺术学院学生，民间知名画家，中国在押政治犯（<span lang="EN-US">CPPC</span>编号：<span lang="EN-US">00704</span>）。曾因两次造访哈萨克国，并其绘画内容主要涉猎浓郁民族特色（即纪念、弘扬哈萨克游牧民族出现过的英雄们，以及具有民族风情的哈萨克毡房和哈萨克草原等），遂于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被新疆伊犁市当局抓走，送当地某再教育营（又称集中营）接受政治学习教育；后被当地警方以不具名罪由转正式逮捕，并被新疆伊犁市法院秘密判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，罪名不清；据悉，其在集中营学习期间已患严重疾病，后在关押密审期间精神失常；其父多次欲探望女儿，均遭到当局拒绝，且无法获悉其实际所患疾病名称及具体所在监狱地址。服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">7</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、范路杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江西九江市法轮功学员。家住江西九江市浔阳区。<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月之后，范路杰被浔阳区公安分局劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次，第一次是<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半；第二次是<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月；第三次是<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年五月被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，总计被劳教<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。三次劳教都是被关押在九江市马家垄劳教所。期间，范路杰一直被包夹，强迫劳动，吃饭、睡觉、上厕所都被人跟着，不许跟其他法轮功学员接触，不准自由说话。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被濂溪区公安分局警察抓捕，一直被关押在九江看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月传出，仅靠一段模糊不清的监控视频，范路杰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">8</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、高小平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东潍坊市昌邑市法轮功学员，在中共对法轮功持续至今近<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年的迫害中，被迫流离失所多年，落脚在聊城市东昌府区。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日与法轮功学员黄焕芝，在散发真相资料时，被李海务派出所警察抓捕，关押在聊城市看守所。于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日高小平被山东聊城法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年零<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，黄焕芝被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。两名善良妇女现已在山东女子监狱服刑。高小平刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">9</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、韩雪松：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省营口市鲅鱼圈区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日中午<span lang="EN-US">11</span>点，法轮功学员金翠香开着松花江小面包车，载着韩雪松（<span lang="EN-US">49</span>岁）、韩美玲（<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁）、柳爱敏（<span lang="EN-US">56</span>岁）、徐笑岩行进在大连瓦房店李官镇的街道上，突然一辆警车拦截，随即围过来六七个警察，在车上搜出两小摞《九评》书。几名法轮功学员被抓捕到李官镇派出所。后刑拘逮捕起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日瓦房店法院判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>位法轮功学员：金翠香<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年并罚款<span lang="EN-US">8000</span>元；韩雪松被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月并罚款<span lang="EN-US">8000</span>元；韩美玲<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年并罚款<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元；柳爱敏<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年并罚款<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元；徐笑岩、柳爱敏已获释。韩雪松刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">10</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、何菊英：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1964</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出生，湖南省宁远县人，湖南省宁远县中和镇上街村村民，维权访民，<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年，曾因其上初中的儿子被学校的几位恶少殴打致残，遭地方法院枉法判决，遂走上了漫长艰辛的维权之路；之后又因其上访的行为触碰了地方当局的利益神经，故而遭到地方当局的严酷打压，并因此屡遭非法关押；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，曾两次因上访维权遭遇政府枉法构陷，被先后处以劳动教养共计<span lang="EN-US">30</span>个月，并被多次关押于精神病院和黑监狱；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，曾因被关在教养所内，其家中老人无人照顾且遭到当局的恶意骚扰和恐吓，致使两位老人在惊吓过度和贫病交加中相继去世。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，当其再次到北京上访时，被地方当局从北京截访并强行遣回原籍，随后被警方以“非法上访”为罪由处以行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，又被以涉嫌“敲诈勒索政府罪”刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被湖南省宁远县检察院以同罪名正式批捕。目前被羁押于湖南省宁远县看守所，后案件音信全无。后获悉遭判刑，已经释放。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">11</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、胡功</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日出生，内蒙古自治区呼和浩特市玉泉区人，原呼和浩特市回民区义和巷“芬芳理发店”理发师，曾被当地报纸誉为“<span lang="EN-US">25</span>年义务理发的好市民”，基督徒，呼和浩特市基督教“呼喊派”召会负责人，中国在押良心犯。曾因信仰有争议的基督教地方召会“呼喊派”，拥有“呼喊派”书籍，并与他人积极散发<span lang="EN-US">800</span>百余份福音宣传资料，触动了中共当局加强意识形态、信仰自由控制的敏感神经，随于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被呼和浩特市玉泉区警方从居住地带走，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被以涉嫌“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”刑事拘留，被关押于内蒙古自治区呼和浩特市第三看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，又被以同罪名正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其涉嫌“邪教案”被内蒙古自治区呼和浩特市玉泉区检察院提起公诉，被控以“小排聚会、主日聚会、婚礼聚会、境外特会进行聚集，通过电子邮件接收境外的邪教资料，与境外的邪教人员进行非法联系”；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，最终被呼和浩特市玉泉区法院以“组织和利用邪教破坏国家法律实施”罪重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年；其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日经呼和浩特市中级法院二审宣判，依然维持原判。目前具体服刑监狱不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、胡水英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江西南昌市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份，南昌市西湖区公安分局与东湖区公安分局联合，成立了迫害法轮功学员的专案组。他们通过摄像头查找后进行抓捕、抄家，分别于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日逐一抓捕了张莉、江兰英、张文涛、胡水英、陈宝芝。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，江西省南昌市西湖区法院判法轮功学员胡水英<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US"> 2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">13</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、黄信：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">安徽省界首市拆迁访民。黄信与界首市其他访民于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月初赴京上访，返回界首市家中于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被警察抓走，并被警方抄走家中的信访资料。当晚<span lang="EN-US">19</span>时黄信被界首市公安局决定以“涉嫌敲诈勒索罪”刑拘，送界首市看守所羁押。据悉黄信就房屋拆迁之事此前起诉界首市东城街道办事处的行政案件一审胜诉。后获悉，已获释。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">14</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、兰桂媛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年过花甲的兰桂媛老人，早在<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年因为举报单位领导贪污腐败、替广大退休职工讨要退休工资，就遭受了罕见的迫害，右腿被警察打残，只能终身拄拐行走，常年在京上访。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，湖南省岳阳市岳阳楼区政府人员，来京劝返兰桂媛。兰桂媛不想树敌过多，顺从了政府人员“一带一路”离开北京的意愿。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">11</span>点左右，六七个不明身份的人闯进了兰桂媛的家中，将兰桂媛强行带走，同时拿走了兰桂媛电脑、手机、上访材料等。到<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日“一带一路”峰会举行前一天，兰桂媛家人收到刑事拘留通知书，称兰桂媛涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”被刑拘。后音信全无。后获悉，已获释。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">15</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、勒智多杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">藏族，<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日生，被捕前居住于青海省果洛州玛沁县雪山乡阳柯河牧委会。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日遭到当局拘留，于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被批捕。 当局指控勒智多杰<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年期间，多次在个人社交网站上转发和发布祝福西藏流亡政府工作人员和西藏精神领袖达赖喇嘛的图文和视频：<span lang="EN-US">1</span>、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，勒智多杰于个人微博上转发祝福西藏流亡政府工作人员新年贺词的图文，该微博被点击次数达<span lang="EN-US">2383</span>次。<span lang="EN-US"> 2</span>、同日，勒智多杰使用微信，在朋友圈中转发<span lang="EN-US">10</span>秒钟的达赖喇嘛新年贺词短视频。<span lang="EN-US"> 3</span>、<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，正值藏区“<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月敏感期”期间，勒智多杰用微博转发<span lang="EN-US">1</span>条网络上出现的被指控含有“藏独”内容的图文。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>、<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，勒智多杰于个人微博上发表了赞扬，祝福西藏精神领袖达赖喇嘛的文字，并配发<span lang="EN-US">1</span>张达赖喇嘛幼年照片。 洛州中级法院判据此处勒智多杰有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。勒智多杰当庭表示不上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">16</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、李常秋：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">四川成都法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，成都市法轮功学员赵帮海、李常秋夫妇因宣传法轮功而被抓捕。后均遭枉判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年有期徒刑，那年他们的独生女儿十六岁。四年来，失去父母照顾的独生女儿多次要求会见冤狱中的父亲，却遭监狱无情的推诿、拒绝。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">17</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、李春华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东省龙口市芦头镇市后乔家村访民。李春华是因为和亲属关于赡养老人、财产分割等问题产生矛盾后起诉至法院，得知判决结果后李春华认为法院判决不公开始逐级上访，因上访曾被关劳教并关精神病院。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日李春华被龙口市公安局以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年的<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被取保候审，因为李春华在取保候审期间没有经过龙口市公安局批准擅自离开龙口市被警方传唤，期间李春华拒不配合警方传唤并和丈夫一起辱骂殴打传唤她的民警，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被龙口市检察院以涉嫌“妨碍公务罪”批准逮捕，于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日起诉到法院，随后龙口市法院决定于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时<span lang="EN-US">30</span>分开庭审理该案。未宣判。后音信全无。后获悉，已判刑，刑满出狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">18</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、李久成：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">内蒙古莫力达瓦旗（莫旗）法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年五十五岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月末，即中共十九大召开的前夕，内蒙古自治区下发命令，莫旗公安局国保大队、“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”非法组织、刑警队、派出所、社区人员假借维稳之名，疯狂地抓捕莫旗法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，李久成被抓捕。李久成被关押一年多后，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被庭审，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月中旬被枉判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。李久成坚持信仰无罪，继续申诉。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">19</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、廖松林</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：生于<span lang="EN-US">1941</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，湖南郴州市军人接待站退休职工，法轮功学员。廖松林<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年被绑架到洗脑班关押；<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月被抓捕，关押在郴州市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被郴州市北湖区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，关押在湖南常德津市监狱。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年又被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，合计已<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年冤刑。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，郴州市北湖区国保大队，在没有出示任何合法手续、证件的情况下，绑架了七十七岁的法轮功学员廖松林。之后，五个警察强行进入廖松林家抄家，将法轮功书籍、九千多元人民币等私人物品全部抄走。随后，廖松林被关押在郴州市看守所。期间，七十七岁高龄的廖松林被医生检测出身患高血压、冠心病、轻微脑梗、肺结核等病症。因此缘故，廖松林被转到一九八医院继续关押。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，湖南省郴州市北湖区法院判处廖松林<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">20</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、陆祚钰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">福建失地农民、维权人士。陆祚钰是福建省屏南县古汾镇长汾村人，一家<span lang="EN-US">8</span>口人共十余亩耕地，靠种植蘑菇和养猪的收入维持生活。到<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年，全家的耕地被政府动用暴力强行征用，一家人还多人被政府雇佣的征地人员打伤，报警公安不予理睬，陆祚钰为此走访各级政府，反映地方政府违法征用耕地的行为，结果是屡屡遭到打击报复，甚至被判刑入狱。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月底因北京上访被拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被行政拘留九天期满，于当日上午八点被公安以“寻衅滋事”立即传唤，并于当天下午三点以口袋罪“寻衅滋事”升级为刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，又遭正式批捕、起诉。羁押于宁德看守所。陆祚钰遭当局构陷寻衅滋事罪案将于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日上午九点在柘荣县法院第一法庭开庭审理，由纪中久律师代理，未当庭宣判。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，陆祚钰被福建柘荣县人民法院以寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，即自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日止。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">21</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、罗丽：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，辽阳法轮功学员李伟涛、王永生、国世游、谷林杰、汤显贺、罗丽被辽阳市白塔公安分局国保警察马文博等人绑架、抄家，当时国世游身体不适被多个警察抬着抓走的。辽宁省辽阳市白塔区法院<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月对李伟涛等六名法轮功学员判刑，刑期是：李伟涛<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、王永生<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罗丽<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、汤显贺<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半、国世游<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、谷林杰<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，并附带罚款，其中五人已上诉。罗丽刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">22</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、钱风林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张家口法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，钱风林女士在康保县县城张文营街上送法轮功台历时，遭国保大队吕正带人抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日上午，遭庭审。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，钱风林被康保县法院一审判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金一万元。钱风林不服判决，上诉到张家口中级法院。上诉被驳回。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">23</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、全世欣：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1976</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日出生，北京市人，北京市海淀区四季青东平庄<span lang="EN-US">56</span>号居民，维权访民，贪腐举报人，网络推友，人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。早年曾因个人宅基地及住房被政府强拆而被迫维权多年，至今仍未获批宅基地或获赔住房，成为无家可归的北京土著农民；在维权过程中，因发现地方干部有严重贪腐现象，并公开向多个职能部门举报，随遭地方当权者严厉打压和非法拘押；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，因使用互联网翻墙软件在推特上发表对中共当局及执政者批评言论，被网警监控发现，而被北京海淀区警方因言获罪，立刻以“寻衅滋事”罪由行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，又因身穿写有“蔡奇见家属”字样的白色短袖<span lang="EN-US">T</span>恤，高喊要求与市政府相关负责人见面递交相关材料，寻求解决问题，而被海淀区警方以“扰乱公共场所秩序”罪由行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，再次被海淀区警方莫名带走，后被以“寻衅滋事”罪由刑拘，好友疑称此与其曾在推特上多次发支持香港“反送中”抗议游行等言论有关；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，其被北京市海淀区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，其被起诉，起诉书称其“自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年注册并使用推特，散布大量虚假信息，严重扰乱社会秩序”，因而触犯刑法，需要提交法院予以审判；据悉，其拒绝官派律师，表示若见不到朋友委托的律师将拒绝出庭。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月开庭后休庭。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被关押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月的北京维权人士全世欣案宣判，全世欣获刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。目前全世欣被羁押于北京市海淀区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">24</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、任秀英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈尔滨市道外区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日哈尔滨市松北区公安分局绑架了<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功学员：石香云、贾艳玲、包义、魏续旺、孔庆艳、朱凤英、赵熙茹、刘君、任秀英、杨骐骥、吴樨、张树霞、宫文义。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被松北区检察院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被哈尔滨市松北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">25</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、石桂尊：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1944</span>年生，黑龙江省佳木斯市法轮功学员，家住佳木斯市前进区康居嘉园，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>十日前开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日晚，佳木斯市前进公安分局和中山派出所的警察及林海社区的协警<span lang="EN-US">1</span>伙人，到佳木斯市前进区康居嘉园，闯入石桂尊老人的家，将石桂尊抓捕，并抄家。石桂尊老人被强行送到佳木斯市看守所关押、构陷。后得知，石桂尊老人已被佳木斯市向阳区法院庭审，并判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，石桂尊被移送到黑龙江省女子监狱刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">26</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、沈爱斌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1973</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日出生，江苏省无锡市人，退伍军人，原无锡市锡山区城管局城管大队长，维权公民，公民记者。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，因与丁红芬、沈果冬等<span lang="EN-US">20</span>余人一起营救被非法拘禁于当地东郊宾馆内“黑监狱”的访民，及时救出<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人（其中包括一位<span lang="EN-US">82</span>岁的老妇人），遂被无锡市滨湖区警方于<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日从家中带走；<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，被当地警方以“涉嫌聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”刑事拘留，并遭到刑讯逼供；<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被警方正式逮捕；后因无锡市滨湖区检察院认定证据不足，两次退侦，于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被取保候审；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日再次因“<span lang="EN-US">2013.6.23</span>营救黑监狱受害人事件”被刑拘，关押在无锡市第一看守所，后被以涉嫌“故意毁坏财物罪”正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被江苏省无锡市滨湖区法院以同罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日刑满出狱后，依然坚持维权，同时累遭当局非法监视、跟踪、拘留及传唤等迫害；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，因无锡市再现<span lang="EN-US">4</span>·<span lang="EN-US">13</span>大抓捕访民事件再次被以涉嫌“故意伤害罪”刑拘<span lang="EN-US">37</span>天，释放后旋即被监视居住；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日因恐其在<span lang="EN-US">G20</span>峰会期间持续维权而被无锡市警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天，同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被警方以涉“寻衅滋事罪”继续刑拘，后被转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被江苏省无锡市滨湖区法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，已刑满释放。此前被羁押于江苏省无锡市第二看守所。获释后仍遭当局持续的迫害打压。沈爱斌于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日 被无锡市公安局梁溪分局以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，被关押在无锡市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月底，取保释放。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">27</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、汤菊章：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">安徽省合肥市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生。原安徽省合肥市康泰医院医生。中共迫害法轮功，汤菊章曾多次被绑架、劳教、判刑关押，受尽酷刑折磨和凌辱。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被合肥市肥东县国保大队抓捕、抄家，后被押往合肥市女子看守所关押；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月底，汤菊章被构陷到合肥市蜀山区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月获悉，汤菊章被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">28</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、王健：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江苏省南京市人，民主维权公民。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日因言获罪遭强迫失踪。后获知遭刑事拘留。近年来，王健深受民主意识的影响，在社会责任感和政治理念的驱使下，积极参与各种维权活动，其行踪遍及黑龙江省建三江、河南省郑州市、湖南省衡阳市、湖北省武汉市、江苏省苏州市等多个城市；曾参与声援山东曲阜的薛明凯父亲死亡案、河南省郑州市的十君子案，并为维权人士赵枫生、圣观法师、黄静怡、张科科律师等被逮事件进行围观声援；由于其频繁出现在维权现场，随遭到当局的嫉恨和打压；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，因到江苏省苏州市声援维权人士、人权捍卫者范木根血拆案庭审，连续到苏州市中级法院围观，随被警方抓至当地派出所关押，次日即被警方刑拘，被关押在南京市江宁看守所；后在取保候审期间再次前往苏州声援范木根案庭审，又被警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，六四敏感日期间，其被南京市警方突然从家中强行带走，并被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式逮捕，且被指涉嫌危害国家安全；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，其案件开庭审理；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，被南京市江宁区法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日经南京市中级法院二审宣判，依然维持原判；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日刑满释放。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，因曾向当地公安部门申请“反对美国发动贸易战”、“支持国家采取一切反制措施”游行示威而被南京市警方带走，次日被刑拘，后又被以“寻衅滋事罪”监视居住<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个半月；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，取保获释。后王健一直相对低调，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日这次遭强迫失踪、刑事拘留原因还不清楚。被羁押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个多月后获释。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">29</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、王建华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省籍人，深圳市西乡万骏汇大厦公司负责人，深圳同城聚会公民，民主宪政追求者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，因王建华与深圳公民邓洪城、肖兵、王威、李南海、马志权、丁岩、董凌鹏、宋立前、黄安阳等<span lang="EN-US">10</span>数人参加同城聚餐，被深圳警方秘密跟踪并且拍照，次日邓洪成、肖兵、王威、李南海、马志权、丁岩、王军等人相继被深圳警方带走，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日下午，王建华亦被深圳市宝安区西乡警方以核实公司职员身份为由带走，其出租房屋遭搜查，自此失联；后经其妻子及律师等多方打探获悉<span lang="EN-US">, </span>其已于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被深圳市警方以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”执行指定居所监视居住；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其代理律师前往西乡派出所询问案件情况，警方称其家属已来询问，其指定居所监视居住通知书已被邮寄。目前被羁押于深圳市第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被以“颠覆国家政权罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">30</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、王莉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁凤城法轮功学员。二零一八年二月一日，吴娟、王莉在赫家沟给当地居民送“福善吉庆”年画和真相书册时，被村长卜井奎恶意举报，被凤城市公安局凤山分局抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，辽宁凤城法轮功学员吴娟、王莉被凤城法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">31</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、王永生：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，辽阳法轮功学员李伟涛、王永生、国世游、谷林杰、汤显贺、罗丽被辽阳市白塔公安分局国保警察马文博等人绑架、抄家，当时国世游身体不适被多个警察抬着抓走的。辽宁省辽阳市白塔区法院<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月对李伟涛等六名法轮功学员判刑，刑期是：李伟涛<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、王永生<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罗丽<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、汤显贺<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半、国世游<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、谷林杰<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，并附带罚款，其中五人已上诉。王永生刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">32</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、吴娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁凤城法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，吴娟、王莉在赫家沟给当地居民送“福善吉庆”年画和真相书册时，被村长卜井奎恶意举报，被凤城市公安局凤山分局武志鹏等多名警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，辽宁凤城法轮功学员吴娟、王莉被凤城法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">33</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、吴伟明：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安徽省合肥市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1957</span>年生。二零零二年曾因修炼法轮功，判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被合肥市瑶海区公安分局站前路派出所抓捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被合肥市蜀山区法院庭审，后被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，罚金两千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">34</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、翟国兴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">天津法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日早晨在天津河东区万新村菜市场讲法轮功，被警察抓捕到东新派出所。当天中午抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月翟国兴被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月关押到天津女子监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">35</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、张圣相：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1993</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，辽宁省沈阳市人，沈阳市沈河区东堡路<span lang="EN-US">801</span>号<span lang="EN-US">352</span>室公民，贴吧常用名：富士山君、堂岛之龙，健身教练，<span lang="EN-US">MAD</span>作者，<span lang="EN-US">S</span>触吧前吧主，动画设计师，恶俗艺术家，音<span lang="EN-US">MAD</span>圈捍卫者，“恶俗维基网站恶势力犯罪集团案”受害人之一，中国在押政治犯。自幼喜欢动漫，但因体重超胖被人耻笑故而性格十分自卑；后又因动漫初期作品遭人嘲笑，随痛下决心到沈阳帝豪斯健身俱乐部<span lang="EN-US">(</span>大悦城店<span lang="EN-US">)</span>健身<span lang="EN-US">2-3</span>年，终见成效，自此信心大增，性格渐入佳境；大学毕业后，曾供职多个职业；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，开始加入恶俗维基网站，很快成为该媒体平台上恶俗动漫兼音乐制作的骨干成员，并在恶俗圈内知名度较高；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，曾因多家“恶俗圈”网站热发习近平之女习明泽、姐夫邓家贵的相关信息（含户籍、照片等个人信息），其所在“恶俗维基”亦将此类信息挂于网上，遂立遭中共当局严厉打压；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-8</span>月，由公安部迅速成立项目组，针对全国该网站会员实施全面大搜捕；抓捕之后，经严格审讯，感觉他们大多年龄尚小且行为基本无罪，故各地警方又将所抓之人纷纷释放；唯独广东省茂名市警方立功心切，声称要给中共建政<span lang="EN-US">70</span>周年献大礼，随移花接木嫁祸“恶俗维基”，把该警局所辖该网站成员（含其在内）尽都抓捕，同时向公安部谎称“破获了一起与反华势力相勾结的恶势力集团大案”；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，其被广东省茂名市警方跨省抓捕，后被暂短指定居所监视居住和刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被茂名市检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">24</span>人“涉恶势力犯罪集团案”在广东省茂名市茂南区法院开庭审理；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，此案<span lang="EN-US">24</span>人均被宣判，张圣相被一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日；因其等多人均表不服，随即上诉；二审维持原判。目前被羁押于佛山市南海区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">36</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、赵帮海：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">四川成都法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，成都市法轮功学员赵帮海、李常秋夫妇因宣传法轮功而被抓捕。后均遭枉判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年有期徒刑，那年他们的独生女儿十六岁。四年来，失去父母照顾的独生女儿多次要求会见冤狱中的父亲，却遭监狱无情的推诿、拒绝。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">37</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、郑旭飞</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：男，<span lang="EN-US">42</span>岁，山东省乳山市下初镇中心学校体育教师，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，郑旭飞曾因宣传法轮功信息而被警方抓捕，在抓捕过程中，因野蛮抓捕，当被警察拖上警车时，他的锁骨已被摔成骨折，之后被送往看守所刑拘。被关押期间，被戴着手铐脚镣<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个多月，并遭毒打和被逼做奴工。<span lang="EN-US">35</span>天后被强迫交<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元钱准予取保候审。因他被无理关押迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年的绩效工资两万元被他所在单位扣除。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，郑旭飞又因宣传法轮功资料而被乳山市警方抓捕，后被乳山市检察院正式批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被乳山市法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”冤判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，山东省威海中级法院二审维持非法，并追加罚款罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">38</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、周显蓉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川西昌市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日下午，被国安抓捕控制后抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，勒索处罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">39</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、靳凤羽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大午集团集团副总经理。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日凌晨，河北大午农牧集团负责人孙大午及其亲属并集团子公司法人等近<span lang="EN-US">30</span>人被警方突击抓捕。其后，包括孙大午妻子刘会茹等部分公司高管，被以“非法吸收公众存款”罪名批捕，而孙大午等其他公司高管以“指定居所监视居住”的方式被采取强制措施。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，河北大午集团此前被“指定居所监视居住”的<span lang="EN-US">7</span>位当事人家属，分别收到公安送达的逮捕通知书。靳凤羽被控罪名：衅滋事罪、聚众冲击国家机关罪。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">16</span>时，大午案经历<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天庭审后当庭宣判：靳凤羽被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月，缓刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。当庭获释。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US" minor-fareast;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size:
